* [Golf](https://github.com/dinever/golf) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dinever/golf?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dinever/golf?style=flat-square) - Golf is a fast, simple and lightweight micro-web framework for Go. It comes with powerful features and has no dependencies other than the Go Standard Library.
* [Gondola](https://github.com/rainycape/gondola) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/rainycape/gondola?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/rainycape/gondola?style=flat-square) - The web framework for writing faster sites, faster.
* [gongular](https://github.com/mustafaakin/gongular) - Fast Go web framework with input mapping/validation and (DI) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mustafaakin/gongular) - Fast Go web framework with input mapping/validation and (DI?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mustafaakin/gongular) - Fast Go web framework with input mapping/validation and (DI?style=flat-square) Dependency Injection.
* [Macaron](https://github.com/go-macaron/macaron) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-macaron/macaron?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-macaron/macaron?style=flat-square) - Macaron is a high productive and modular design web framework in Go.
* [mango](https://github.com/paulbellamy/mango) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/paulbellamy/mango?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/paulbellamy/mango?style=flat-square) - Mango is a modular web-application framework for Go, inspired by Rack, and PEP333.
* [Microservice](https://github.com/claygod/microservice) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/claygod/microservice?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/claygod/microservice?style=flat-square) - The framework for the creation of microservices, written in Golang.
* [neo](https://github.com/ivpusic/neo) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/ivpusic/neo?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/ivpusic/neo?style=flat-square) - Neo is minimal and fast Go Web Framework with extremely simple API.
* [Resoursea](https://github.com/resoursea/api) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/resoursea/api?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/resoursea/api?style=flat-square) - REST framework for quickly writing resource based services.
* [REST Layer](http://rest-layer.io) - Framework to build REST/GraphQL API on top of databases with mostly configuration over code.
* [Revel](https://github.com/revel/revel) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/revel/revel?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/revel/revel?style=flat-square) - High-productivity web framework for the Go language.
* [rex](https://github.com/goanywhere/rex) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/goanywhere/rex?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/goanywhere/rex?style=flat-square) - Rex is a library for modular development built upon gorilla/mux, fully compatible with `net/http`.
* [sawsij](https://github.com/jaybill/sawsij) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/jaybill/sawsij?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/jaybill/sawsij?style=flat-square) - lightweight, open-source web framework for building high-performance, data-driven web applications.
* [tango](https://github.com/lunny/tango) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/lunny/tango?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/lunny/tango?style=flat-square) - Micro & pluggable web framework for Go.
* [tigertonic](https://github.com/rcrowley/go-tigertonic) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/rcrowley/go-tigertonic?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/rcrowley/go-tigertonic?style=flat-square) - Go framework for building JSON web services inspired by Dropwizard.
* [traffic](https://github.com/pilu/traffic) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/pilu/traffic?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/pilu/traffic?style=flat-square) - Sinatra inspired regexp/pattern mux and web framework for Go.
* [utron](https://github.com/gernest/utron) - Lightweight MVC framework for Go(Golang) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gernest/utron) - Lightweight MVC framework for Go(Golang?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gernest/utron) - Lightweight MVC framework for Go(Golang?style=flat-square).
* [violetear](https://github.com/nbari/violetear) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/nbari/violetear?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/nbari/violetear?style=flat-square) - Go HTTP router.
* [YARF](https://github.com/yarf-framework/yarf) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/yarf-framework/yarf?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/yarf-framework/yarf?style=flat-square) - Fast micro-framework designed to build REST APIs and web services in a fast and simple way.
* [Zerver](https://github.com/cosiner/zerver) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/cosiner/zerver?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/cosiner/zerver?style=flat-square) - Zerver is an expressive, modular, feature completed RESTful framework.

### Middlewares

#### Actual middlewares

* [CORS](https://github.com/rs/cors) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/rs/cors?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/rs/cors?style=flat-square) - Easily add CORS capabilities to your API.
* [formjson](https://github.com/rs/formjson) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/rs/formjson?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/rs/formjson?style=flat-square) - Transparently handle JSON input as a standard form POST.
* [Limiter](https://github.com/ulule/limiter) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/ulule/limiter?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/ulule/limiter?style=flat-square) - Dead simple rate limit middleware for Go.
* [Tollbooth](https://github.com/didip/tollbooth) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/didip/tollbooth?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/didip/tollbooth?style=flat-square) - Rate limit HTTP request handler.
* [XFF](https://github.com/sebest/xff) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/sebest/xff?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/sebest/xff?style=flat-square) - Handle `X-Forwarded-For` header and friends.

#### Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

* [alice](https://github.com/justinas/alice) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/justinas/alice?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/justinas/alice?style=flat-square) - Painless middleware chaining for Go.
* [catena](https://github.com/codemodus/catena) - http.Handler wrapper catenation (same API as "chain") [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/codemodus/catena) - http.Handler wrapper catenation (same API as "chain"?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/codemodus/catena) - http.Handler wrapper catenation (same API as "chain"?style=flat-square).
* [chain](https://github.com/codemodus/chain) - Handler wrapper chaining with scoped data (net/context-based "middleware") [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/codemodus/chain) - Handler wrapper chaining with scoped data (net/context-based "middleware"?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/codemodus/chain) - Handler wrapper chaining with scoped data (net/context-based "middleware"?style=flat-square).
* [go-wrap](https://github.com/go-on/wrap) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-on/wrap?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-on/wrap?style=flat-square) - Small middlewares package for net/http.
* [gores](https://github.com/alioygur/gores) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/alioygur/gores?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/alioygur/gores?style=flat-square) - Go package that handles HTML, JSON, XML and etc. responses. Useful for RESTful APIs.
* [interpose](https://github.com/carbocation/interpose) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/carbocation/interpose?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/carbocation/interpose?style=flat-square) - Minimalist net/http middleware for golang.
* [muxchain](https://github.com/stephens2424/muxchain) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/stephens2424/muxchain?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/stephens2424/muxchain?style=flat-square) - Lightweight middleware for net/http.
* [negroni](https://github.com/urfave/negroni) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/urfave/negroni?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/urfave/negroni?style=flat-square) - Idiomatic HTTP middleware for Golang.
* [render](https://github.com/unrolled/render) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/unrolled/render?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/unrolled/render?style=flat-square) - Go package for easily rendering JSON, XML, and HTML template responses.
* [rye](https://github.com/InVisionApp/rye) - Tiny Go middleware library (with canned Middlewares) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/InVisionApp/rye) - Tiny Go middleware library (with canned Middlewares?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/InVisionApp/rye) - Tiny Go middleware library (with canned Middlewares?style=flat-square) that supports JWT, CORS, Statsd, and Go 1.7 context.
* [stats](https://github.com/thoas/stats) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/thoas/stats?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/thoas/stats?style=flat-square) - Go middleware that stores various information about your web application.
* [Volatile](https://github.com/volatile/core) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/volatile/core?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/volatile/core?style=flat-square) - Minimalist middleware stack promoting flexibility, good practices and clean code.

### Routers

* [alien](https://github.com/gernest/alien) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gernest/alien?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gernest/alien?style=flat-square) - Lightweight and fast http router from outer space.
* [Bone](https://github.com/go-zoo/bone) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-zoo/bone?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-zoo/bone?style=flat-square) - Lightning Fast HTTP Multiplexer.
* [Bxog](https://github.com/claygod/Bxog) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/claygod/Bxog?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/claygod/Bxog?style=flat-square) - Simple and fast HTTP router for Go. It works with routes of varying difficulty, length and nesting. And he knows how to create a URL from the received parameters.
* [chi](https://github.com/go-chi/chi) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-chi/chi?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-chi/chi?style=flat-square) - Small, fast and expressive HTTP router built on net/context.
* [fasthttprouter](https://github.com/buaazp/fasthttprouter) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/buaazp/fasthttprouter?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/buaazp/fasthttprouter?style=flat-square) - High performance router forked from `httprouter`. The first router fit for `fasthttp`.
* [gocraft/web](https://github.com/gocraft/web) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gocraft/web?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gocraft/web?style=flat-square) - Mux and middleware package in Go.
* [Goji](https://github.com/goji/goji) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/goji/goji?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/goji/goji?style=flat-square) - Goji is a minimalistic and flexible HTTP request multiplexer with support for `net/context`.
* [GoRouter](https://github.com/vardius/gorouter) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/vardius/gorouter?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/vardius/gorouter?style=flat-square) - GoRouter is a Server/API micro framwework, HTTP request router, multiplexer, mux that provides request router with middleware supporting `net/context`.
* [gowww/router](https://github.com/gowww/router) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gowww/router?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gowww/router?style=flat-square) - Lightning fast HTTP router fully compatible with the net/http.Handler interface.
* [httprouter](https://github.com/julienschmidt/httprouter) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/julienschmidt/httprouter?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/julienschmidt/httprouter?style=flat-square) - High performance router. Use this and the standard http handlers to form a very high performance web framework.
* [httptreemux](https://github.com/dimfeld/httptreemux) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dimfeld/httptreemux?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dimfeld/httptreemux?style=flat-square) - High-speed, flexible tree-based HTTP router for Go. Inspiration from httprouter.
* [lars](https://github.com/go-playground/lars) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-playground/lars?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-playground/lars?style=flat-square) - Is a lightweight, fast and extensible zero allocation HTTP router for Go used to create customizable frameworks.
* [medeina](https://github.com/imdario/medeina) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/imdario/medeina?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/imdario/medeina?style=flat-square) - Medeina is a HTTP routing tree based on HttpRouter, inspired by Roda and Cuba.
* [mux](https://github.com/gorilla/mux) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gorilla/mux?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gorilla/mux?style=flat-square) - Powerful URL router and dispatcher for golang.
* [ozzo-routing](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-routing) - An extremely fast Go (golang) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-routing) - An extremely fast Go (golang?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-routing) - An extremely fast Go (golang?style=flat-square) HTTP router that supports regular expression route matching. Comes with full support for building RESTful APIs.
* [pat](https://github.com/bmizerany/pat) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/bmizerany/pat?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/bmizerany/pat?style=flat-square) - Sinatra style pattern muxer for Gos net/http library, by the author of Sinatra.
* [pure](https://github.com/go-playground/pure) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-playground/pure?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/go-playground/pure?style=flat-square) - Is a lightweight HTTP router that sticks to the std "net/http" implementation.
* [Siesta](https://github.com/VividCortex/siesta) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/VividCortex/siesta?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/VividCortex/siesta?style=flat-square) - Composable framework to write middleware and handlers.
* [vestigo](https://github.com/husobee/vestigo) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/husobee/vestigo?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/husobee/vestigo?style=flat-square) - Performant, stand-alone, HTTP compliant URL Router for go web applications.
* [xmux](https://github.com/rs/xmux) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/rs/xmux?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/rs/xmux?style=flat-square) - High performance muxer based on `httprouter` with `net/context` support.
* [zeus](https://github.com/daryl/zeus) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/daryl/zeus?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/daryl/zeus?style=flat-square) - Very simple and fast HTTP router for Go.

## Windows

* [d3d9](https://github.com/gonutz/d3d9) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gonutz/d3d9?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gonutz/d3d9?style=flat-square) - Go bindings for Direct3D9.

## XML

*Libraries and tools for manipulating XML.*

* [go-pkg-xmlx](https://github.com/jteeuwen/go-pkg-xmlx) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/jteeuwen/go-pkg-xmlx?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/jteeuwen/go-pkg-xmlx?style=flat-square) - Extension to the standard Go XML package. Maintains a node tree that allows forward/backwards browsing and exposes some simple single/multi-node search functions.
* [XML-Comp](https://github.com/xml-comp/xml-comp) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/xml-comp/xml-comp?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/xml-comp/xml-comp?style=flat-square) - Simple command line XML comparer that generates diffs of folders, files and tags.
* [xmlwriter](https://github.com/shabbyrobe/xmlwriter) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/shabbyrobe/xmlwriter?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/shabbyrobe/xmlwriter?style=flat-square) - Procedural XML generation API based on libxml2's xmlwriter module.
* [xpath](https://github.com/antchfx/xpath) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/antchfx/xpath?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/antchfx/xpath?style=flat-square) - XPath package for Go.
* [xquery](https://github.com/antchfx/xquery) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/antchfx/xquery?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/antchfx/xquery?style=flat-square) - XQuery lets you extract data from HTML/XML documents using XPath expression.

# Tools

*Go software and plugins.*

## Code Analysis

* [apicompat](https://github.com/bradleyfalzon/apicompat) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/bradleyfalzon/apicompat?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/bradleyfalzon/apicompat?style=flat-square) - Checks recent changes to a Go project for backwards incompatible changes.
* [dupl](https://github.com/mibk/dupl) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mibk/dupl?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mibk/dupl?style=flat-square) - Tool for code clone detection.
* [errcheck](https://github.com/kisielk/errcheck) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/kisielk/errcheck?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/kisielk/errcheck?style=flat-square) - Errcheck is a program for checking for unchecked errors in Go programs.
* [gcvis](https://github.com/davecheney/gcvis) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/davecheney/gcvis?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/davecheney/gcvis?style=flat-square) - Visualise Go program GC trace data in real time.
* [Go Metalinter](https://github.com/alecthomas/gometalinter) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/alecthomas/gometalinter?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/alecthomas/gometalinter?style=flat-square) - Metalinter is a tool to automatically apply all static analysis tool and report their output in normalized form.
* [go-checkstyle](https://github.com/qiniu/checkstyle) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/qiniu/checkstyle?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/qiniu/checkstyle?style=flat-square) - checkstyle is a style check tool like java checkstyle. This tool inspired by java checkstyle, golint. The style refered to some points in Go Code Review Comments.
* [go-cleanarch](https://github.com/roblaszczak/go-cleanarch) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/roblaszczak/go-cleanarch?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/roblaszczak/go-cleanarch?style=flat-square) - go-cleanarch was created to validate Clean Architecture rules, like a The Dependency Rule and interaction between packages in your Go projects.
* [go-outdated](https://github.com/firstrow/go-outdated) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/firstrow/go-outdated?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/firstrow/go-outdated?style=flat-square) - Console application that displays outdated packages.
* [goast-viewer](https://github.com/yuroyoro/goast-viewer) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/yuroyoro/goast-viewer?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/yuroyoro/goast-viewer?style=flat-square) - Web based Golang AST visualizer.
* [GoCover.io](http://gocover.io/) - GoCover.io offers the code coverage of any golang package as a service.
* [goimports](https://godoc.org/golang.org/x/tools/cmd/goimports) - Tool to fix (add, remove) your Go imports automatically.
* [GoLint](https://github.com/golang/lint) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/golang/lint?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/golang/lint?style=flat-square) - Golint is a linter for Go source code.
* [Golint online](http://go-lint.appspot.com/) - Lints online Go source files on GitHub, Bitbucket and Google Project Hosting using the golint package.
* [goreturns](https://sourcegraph.com/github.com/sqs/goreturns) - Adds zero-value return statements to match the func return types.
* [gosimple](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/gosimple) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/gosimple?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/gosimple?style=flat-square) - gosimple is a linter for Go source code that specialises on simplifying code.
* [gostatus](https://github.com/shurcooL/gostatus) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/shurcooL/gostatus?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/shurcooL/gostatus?style=flat-square) - Command line tool, shows the status of repositories that contain Go packages.
* [interfacer](https://github.com/mvdan/interfacer) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mvdan/interfacer?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mvdan/interfacer?style=flat-square) - Linter that suggests interface types.
* [lint](https://github.com/surullabs/lint) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/surullabs/lint?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/surullabs/lint?style=flat-square) - Run linters as part of go test.
* [staticcheck](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/staticcheck) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/staticcheck?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/staticcheck?style=flat-square) - staticcheck is `go vet` on steroids, applying a ton of static analysis checks you might be used to from tools like ReSharper for C#.
* [unconvert](https://github.com/mdempsky/unconvert) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mdempsky/unconvert?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mdempsky/unconvert?style=flat-square) - Remove unnecessary type conversions from Go source.
* [unused](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/unused) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/unused?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/unused?style=flat-square) - unused checks Go code for unused constants, variables, functions and types.
* [validate](https://github.com/mccoyst/validate) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mccoyst/validate?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mccoyst/validate?style=flat-square) - Automatically validates struct fields with tags.

* [DDNS](https://github.com/skibish/ddns) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/skibish/ddns?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/skibish/ddns?style=flat-square) - Personal DDNS client with Digital Ocean Networking DNS as backend.
* [Docker](http://www.docker.com/) - Open platform for distributed applications for developers and sysadmins.
* [Documize](https://github.com/documize/community) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/documize/community?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/documize/community?style=flat-square) - Modern wiki software that integrates data from SaaS tools.
* [fleet](https://github.com/coreos/fleet) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/coreos/fleet?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/coreos/fleet?style=flat-square) - Distributed init System.
* [Go Package Store](https://github.com/shurcooL/Go-Package-Store) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/shurcooL/Go-Package-Store?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/shurcooL/Go-Package-Store?style=flat-square) - App that displays updates for the Go packages in your GOPATH.
* [gocc](https://github.com/goccmack/gocc) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/goccmack/gocc?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/goccmack/gocc?style=flat-square) - Gocc is a compiler kit for Go written in Go.
* [GoDocTooltip](https://github.com/diankong/GoDocTooltip) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/diankong/GoDocTooltip?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/diankong/GoDocTooltip?style=flat-square) - Chrome extension for Go Doc sites, which shows function description as tooltip at funciton list.
* [Gogland](https://jetbrains.com/go) - Full featured cross-platform Go IDE.
* [Gor](https://github.com/buger/gor) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/buger/gor?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/buger/gor?style=flat-square) - Http traffic replication tool, for replaying traffic from production to stage/dev environments in real-time.
* [hugo](http://gohugo.io/) - Fast and Modern Static Website Engine.
* [ide](https://github.com/thestrukture/ide) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/thestrukture/ide?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/thestrukture/ide?style=flat-square) - Browser accessible IDE. Designed for Go with Go.
* [ipe](https://github.com/dimiro1/ipe) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dimiro1/ipe?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/dimiro1/ipe?style=flat-square) - Open source Pusher server implementation compatible with Pusher client libraries written in GO.
* [JayDiff](https://github.com/yazgazan/jaydiff) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/yazgazan/jaydiff?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/yazgazan/jaydiff?style=flat-square) - JSON diff utility written in Go.
* [Juju](https://jujucharms.com/) - Cloud-agnostic service deployment and orchestration - supports EC2, Azure, Openstack, MAAS and more.
* [Leaps](https://github.com/jeffail/leaps) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/jeffail/leaps?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/jeffail/leaps?style=flat-square) - Pair programming service using Operational Transforms.
* [limetext](http://limetext.org/) - Lime Text is a powerful and elegant text editor primarily developed in Go that aims to be a Free and open-source software successor to Sublime Text.
* [LiteIDE](https://github.com/visualfc/liteide) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/visualfc/liteide?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/visualfc/liteide?style=flat-square) - LiteIDE is a simple, open source, cross-platform Go IDE.
* [mockingjay](https://github.com/quii/mockingjay-server) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/quii/mockingjay-server?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/quii/mockingjay-server?style=flat-square) - Fake HTTP servers and consumer driven contracts from one configuration file. You can also make the server randomly misbehave to help do more realistic performance tests.
* [myLG](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/mylg) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mehrdadrad/mylg?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mehrdadrad/mylg?style=flat-square) - Command Line Network Diagnostic tool written in Go.
* [naclpipe](https://github.com/unix4fun/naclpipe) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/unix4fun/naclpipe?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/unix4fun/naclpipe?style=flat-square) - Simple NaCL EC25519 based crypto pipe tool written in Go.
* [nes](https://github.com/fogleman/nes) - Nintendo Entertainment System (NES) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/fogleman/nes) - Nintendo Entertainment System (NES?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/fogleman/nes) - Nintendo Entertainment System (NES?style=flat-square) emulator written in Go.
* [orange-cat](https://github.com/noraesae/orange-cat) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/noraesae/orange-cat?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/noraesae/orange-cat?style=flat-square) - Markdown previewer written in Go.
* [Orbit](https://github.com/gulien/orbit) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gulien/orbit?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/gulien/orbit?style=flat-square) - A simple tool for running commands and generating files from templates.
* [peg](https://github.com/pointlander/peg) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/pointlander/peg?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/pointlander/peg?style=flat-square) - Peg, Parsing Expression Grammar, is an implementation of a Packrat parser generator.
* [Postman](https://github.com/zachlatta/postman) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/zachlatta/postman?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/zachlatta/postman?style=flat-square) - Command-line utility for batch-sending email.
* [restic](https://github.com/restic/restic) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/restic/restic?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/restic/restic?style=flat-square) - De-duplicating backup program.
* [rkt](https://github.com/coreos/rkt) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/coreos/rkt?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/coreos/rkt?style=flat-square) - App Container runtime that integrates with init systems, is compatible with other container formats like Docker, and supports alternative execution engines like KVM.
* [Seaweed File System](https://github.com/chrislusf/seaweedfs) - Fast, Simple and Scalable Distributed File System with O(1) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/chrislusf/seaweedfs) - Fast, Simple and Scalable Distributed File System with O(1?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/chrislusf/seaweedfs) - Fast, Simple and Scalable Distributed File System with O(1?style=flat-square) disk seek.
* [shell2http](https://github.com/msoap/shell2http) - Executing shell commands via http server (for prototyping or remote control) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/msoap/shell2http) - Executing shell commands via http server (for prototyping or remote control?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/msoap/shell2http) - Executing shell commands via http server (for prototyping or remote control?style=flat-square).
* [snap](https://github.com/intelsdi-x/snap) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/intelsdi-x/snap?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/intelsdi-x/snap?style=flat-square) - Powerful telemetry framework.
* [Stack Up](https://github.com/pressly/sup) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/pressly/sup?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/pressly/sup?style=flat-square) - Stack Up, a super simple deployment tool - just Unix - think of it like 'make' for a network of servers.
* [syncthing](https://syncthing.net/) - Open, decentralized file synchronization tool and protocol.
* [Tenyks](https://github.com/kyleterry/tenyks) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/kyleterry/tenyks?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/kyleterry/tenyks?style=flat-square) - Service oriented IRC bot using Redis and JSON for messaging.
* [toto](https://github.com/blogcin/ToTo) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/blogcin/ToTo?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/blogcin/ToTo?style=flat-square) - Simple proxy server written in Go language, can be used together with browser.
* [toxiproxy](https://github.com/shopify/toxiproxy) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/shopify/toxiproxy?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/shopify/toxiproxy?style=flat-square) - Proxy to simulate network and system conditions for automated tests.
* [tsuru](https://tsuru.io/) - Extensible and open source Platform as a Service software.
* [vFlow](https://github.com/VerizonDigital/vflow) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/VerizonDigital/vflow?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/VerizonDigital/vflow?style=flat-square) - High-performance, scalable and reliable IPFIX, sFlow and Netflow collector.
* [websysd](https://github.com/ian-kent/websysd) - Web based process manager (like Marathon or Upstart) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/ian-kent/websysd) - Web based process manager (like Marathon or Upstart?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/ian-kent/websysd) - Web based process manager (like Marathon or Upstart?style=flat-square).

# Resources

*Where to discover new Go libraries.*

## Benchmarks

* [autobench](https://github.com/davecheney/autobench) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/davecheney/autobench?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/davecheney/autobench?style=flat-square) - Framework to compare the performance between different Go versions.
* [go-benchmark-app](https://github.com/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app?style=flat-square) - Powerful HTTP-benchmark tool mixed with b, Wrk, Siege tools. Gathering statistics and various parameters for benchmarks and comparison results.
* [go-benchmarks](https://github.com/tylertreat/go-benchmarks) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/tylertreat/go-benchmarks?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/tylertreat/go-benchmarks?style=flat-square) - Few miscellaneous Go microbenchmarks. Compare some language features to alternative approaches.
* [go-http-routing-benchmark](https://github.com/julienschmidt/go-http-routing-benchmark) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/julienschmidt/go-http-routing-benchmark?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/julienschmidt/go-http-routing-benchmark?style=flat-square) - Go HTTP request router benchmark and comparison.
* [go-type-assertion-benchmark](https://github.com/hgfischer/go-type-assertion-benchmark) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/hgfischer/go-type-assertion-benchmark?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/hgfischer/go-type-assertion-benchmark?style=flat-square) - Naive performance test of two ways to do type assertion in Go.
* [go-web-framework-benchmark](https://github.com/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark?style=flat-square) - Go web framework benchmark.
* [go_serialization_benchmarks](https://github.com/alecthomas/go_serialization_benchmarks) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/alecthomas/go_serialization_benchmarks?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/alecthomas/go_serialization_benchmarks?style=flat-square) - Benchmarks of Go serialization methods.
* [gocostmodel](https://github.com/PuerkitoBio/gocostmodel) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/PuerkitoBio/gocostmodel?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/PuerkitoBio/gocostmodel?style=flat-square) - Benchmarks of common basic operations for the Go language.
* [golang-micro-benchmarks](https://github.com/amscanne/golang-micro-benchmarks) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/amscanne/golang-micro-benchmarks?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/amscanne/golang-micro-benchmarks?style=flat-square) - Tiny collection of Go micro benchmarks. The intent is to compare some language features to others.
* [golang-sql-benchmark](https://github.com/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark?style=flat-square) - Collection of benchmarks for popular Go database/SQL utilities.
* [gospeed](https://github.com/feyeleanor/GoSpeed) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/feyeleanor/GoSpeed?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/feyeleanor/GoSpeed?style=flat-square) - Go micro-benchmarks for calculating the speed of language constructs.
* [kvbench](https://github.com/jimrobinson/kvbench) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/jimrobinson/kvbench?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/jimrobinson/kvbench?style=flat-square) - Key/Value database benchmark.
* [skynet](https://github.com/atemerev/skynet) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/atemerev/skynet?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/atemerev/skynet?style=flat-square) - Skynet 1M threads microbenchmark.
* [speedtest-resize](https://github.com/fawick/speedtest-resize) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/fawick/speedtest-resize?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/fawick/speedtest-resize?style=flat-square) - Compare various Image resize algorithms for the Go language.

### Tutorials

* [A Tour of Go](http://tour.golang.org/) - Interactive tour of Go.
* [Build web application with Golang](https://github.com/astaxie/build-web-application-with-golang) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/astaxie/build-web-application-with-golang?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/astaxie/build-web-application-with-golang?style=flat-square) - Golang ebook intro how to build a web app with golang.
* [Building Go Web Applications and Microservices Using Gin](https://semaphoreci.com/community/tutorials/building-go-web-applications-and-microservices-using-gin) - Get familiar with Gin and find out how it can help you reduce boilerplate code and build a request handling pipeline.
* [Go By Example](https://gobyexample.com/) - Hands-on introduction to Go using annotated example programs.
* [Go Cheat Sheet](https://github.com/a8m/go-lang-cheat-sheet) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/a8m/go-lang-cheat-sheet?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/a8m/go-lang-cheat-sheet?style=flat-square) - Go's reference card.
* [Go database/sql tutorial](http://go-database-sql.org/) - Introduction to database/sql.
* [Golangbot](https://golangbot.com/learn-golang-series/) - Tutorials to get started with programming in Go.
* [How to Use Godog for Behavior-driven Development in Go](https://semaphoreci.com/community/tutorials/how-to-use-godog-for-behavior-driven-development-in-go) - Get started with Godog  a Behavior-driven development framework for building and testing Go applications.
* [Working with Go](https://github.com/mkaz/working-with-go) [![goreport](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mkaz/working-with-go?style=flat-square])](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/mkaz/working-with-go?style=flat-square) - Intro to go for experienced programmers.
